    name VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,
    contact_number VARCHAR(15),
    organization_id INT,
    FOREIGN KEY (organization_id) REFERENCES nonprofit.organization(organization_id)
);

    organization_id INT PRIMARY KEY,
    name VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,
    mission_statement TEXT
